class="axp-global-header__dls__margin1Lr___2b0On"><span>Singapore</span></span><a class="axp-global-header__dls__displayBlock___9lg9q axp-global-header__dls__pad1T___3Pg-P" element="nav_" id="skipToContent"></div><script async="" src="https://www.aexp-static.com/cdaas/akamai/one/statics/@americanexpress/trackit/1.1.1/package/dist/trackit.js" type="text/javascript"></script><script async="" src="https://www.aexp-static.com/cdaas/one/rum-telemetry/0.3.0.js" type="text/javascript"></script><script type="text/javascript">(function navScript() {
  var nav = function () {
    return {
      isLoggedIn: function isLoggedIn() {
        var amexSessionCookie = nav.readCookie('amexsessioncookie');
        var blueboxCookie = nav.readCookie('blueboxvalues');
        var smSessionCookie = nav.readCookie('SMSESSION');
        var authenticated = false;
        if (amexSessionCookie !== null && amexSessionCookie !== '') {
          var timeNow = new Date().getTime();
          var match = /uts=([^|]+)/.exec(amexSessionCookie);
          if (!match) {
            return false;
          }
          var cookieTimestamp = parseInt(match[1], 10);
          var diff = (timeNow - cookieTimestamp) / (1000 * 60);
          if (diff < 10.1) {
            authenticated = true;
          }
        } else if (blueboxCookie !== null && blueboxCookie !== '' || smSessionCookie !== null && smSessionCookie !== 'LOGGEDOFF') {
          authenticated = true;
        }
        return authenticated;
      },
      readCookie: function readCookie(cookieName) {
        var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
        var cookieIdxStr = cookieName + '=';
        var cookieValue = null;

        for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i += 1) {
          var cookie = cookies[i];
          var cookieStr = cookie.trim();
          if (cookieStr.indexOf(cookieIdxStr) === 0) {
            cookieValue = cookieStr.substring(cookieIdxStr.length, cookieStr.length);
            break;
          }
        }
        return cookieValue;
      },
      toggleLink: function toggleLink() {
        try {
          if (nav.isLoggedIn()) {
            document.getElementById('gnav_logout').style.display = 'inline-block';
            document.getElementById('gnav_login').style.display = 'none';
          } else {
            document.getElementById('gnav_logout').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('gnav_login').style.display = 'inline-block';
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.warn(e);
        }
      }
    };
  }();
  nav.toggleLink();
  return nav;
})();</script></div>
